The application will process local datasets consisting of image sequences, ground truth bounding box JSON files, and model prediction JSON files (containing bounding boxes, classes, and confidence scores). It provides two core views: a statistics dashboard displaying per-class detection metrics (recall, false positive rate, etc.) and an image-by-image comparison view showing visual overlays of ground truth and predicted bounding boxes with distinct visual indicators for correct detections, false positives, and missed detections. The tool prioritizes intuitive visualization, accurate metric calculation, and seamless local file handling.\n     7→  </overview>\n     8→\n     9→  <technology_stack>\n    10→    <frontend>\n    11→      <framework>Vanilla HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript (ES6+)</framework>\n    12→      <styling>Custom CSS with Flexbox/Grid, optional Bootstrap 5 (via CDN) for responsive layout</styling>\n    13→      <visualization>Chart.js (CDN) for statistical charts, Canvas API for bounding box rendering</visualization>\n    14→      <file_handling>FileReader API for local file processing</file_handling>\n    15→      <routing>Client-side routing with JavaScript (hash-based) for page navigation</routing>\n    16→      <icons>Font Awesome (CDN) for visual indicators (check, cross, dash)</icons>\n    17→    </frontend>\n    18→    <backend>\n    19→      <runtime>Python 3.8+</runtime>\n    20→      <framework>Flask 2.0+</framework>\n    21→      <data_processing>\n    22→        - JSON parsing with built-in json module\n    23→        - Image processing with Pillow (PIL) for thumbnail generation\n    24→        - Metric calculation (recall, precision, FPR) with numpy\n    25→      </data_processing>\n    26→      <cors>Flask-CORS for cross-origin resource sharing</cors>\n    27→      <file_management>Built-in os/pathlib for local file system interaction</file_management>\n    28→    </backend>\n    29→    <communication>\n    30→      <api>RESTful endpoints for data processing and retrieval</api>\n    31→      <data_format>JSON for all data exchange between frontend and backend</data_format>\n    32→      <file_upload>Multipart/form-data for batch file upload (optional) or local file path specification</file_handling>\n    33→    </communication>\n    34→    <dependencies>\n    35→      <python>\n    36→        - All images in a single directory (JPG/PNG format) with consistent naming convention (e.g., img_001.jpg, img_002.png)\n    62→        - Image dimensions consistent or variable (tool should handle both)\n    63→      </image_sequence>\n    64→      <ground_truth_json>\n    65→        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001.json)\n    66→        - Structure: {\n    67→            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n    68→            \"width\": 1920,\n    69→            \"height\": 1080,\n    70→            \"annotations\": [\n    71→              {\n    72→                \"class\": \"car\",\n    73→                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2]  # pixel coordinates (top-left, bottom-right)\n    74→              },\n    75→              ...\n    76→            ]\n    77→          }\n    78→      </ground_truth_json>\n    79→      <prediction_json>\n    80→        - Local dataset path configuration (input field for directory path)\n   101→      - Validation of dataset structure (check for images, GT JSON, prediction JSON)\n   102→      - Batch parsing of all files in the dataset directory\n   103→      - Error handling for missing files, invalid JSON formats, and mismatched filenames\n   104→      - Thumbnail generation for all images (150x150px, aspect ratio preserved)\n   105→      - Caching of parsed data to avoid reprocessing on page refresh\n   106→    </file_handling>\n   107→\n   108→    <statistics_dashboard>\n   109→      <metrics_calculation>\n   110→        - **Recall (True Positive Rate)**: TP / (TP + FN) per class\n   111→        - **Precision**: TP / (TP + FP) per class\n   112→        - **False Positive Rate (FPR)**: FP / (FP + TN) per class\n   113→        - **F1 Score**: 2 * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall) per class\n   114→        - **Overall Accuracy**: (TP + TN) / (TP + TN + FP + FN)\n   115→        - **Average Precision (AP)** per class (optional)\n   116→        - **Intersection over Union (IoU)** threshold configuration (default: 0.5) for TP/FP/FN classification\n   117→      </metrics_calculation>\n   118→      <visualization>\n   119→        - Bar charts for per-class recall, precision, FPR\n   120→        - Pie charts for class distribution in ground truth vs predictions\n   121→        - Summary table with all metrics for easy comparison\n   122→        - Sortable and filterable metric table (by class name, metric value)\n   123→        - Export statistics to CSV/JSON format\n   124→        - Interactive tooltips on charts showing exact metric values\n   125→      </visualization>\n   126→      <user_interface>\n   127→        - Dropdown for IoU threshold adjustment (0.3 to 0.9 in 0.1 increments)\n   128→        - Class filter (show/hide specific classes in charts/tables)\n   129→        - Confidence score threshold filter for predictions (0.0 to 1.0 slider)\n   130→        - Reset filters button to restore default settings\n   131→        - The application will process local datasets consisting of image sequences, ground truth bounding box JSON files, and model prediction JSON files (containing bounding boxes, classes, and confidence scores). It provides two core views: a statistics dashboard displaying per-class detection metrics (recall, false positive rate, etc.) and an image-by-image comparison view showing visual overlays of ground truth and predicted bounding boxes with distinct visual indicators for correct detections, false positives, and missed detections. The tool prioritizes intuitive visualization, accurate metric calculation, and seamless local file handling.\n  </overview>\n\n  <technology_stack>\n    <frontend>\n      <framework>Vanilla HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript (ES6+)</framework>\n      <styling>Custom CSS with Flexbox/Grid, optional Bootstrap 5 (via CDN) for responsive layout</styling>\n      <visualization>Chart.js (CDN) for statistical charts, Canvas API for bounding box rendering</visualization>\n      <file_handling>FileReader API for local file processing</file_handling>\n      <routing>Client-side routing with JavaScript (hash-based) for page navigation</routing>\n      <icons>Font Awesome (CDN) for visual indicators (check, cross, dash)</icons>\n    </frontend>\n    <backend>\n      <runtime>Python 3.8+</runtime>\n      <framework>Flask 2.0+</framework>\n      <data_processing>\n        - JSON parsing with built-in json module\n        - Image processing with Pillow (PIL) for thumbnail generation\n        - Metric calculation (recall, precision, FPR) with numpy\n      </data_processing>\n      <cors>Flask-CORS for cross-origin resource sharing</cors>\n      <file_management>Built-in os/pathlib for local file system interaction</file_management>\n    </backend>\n    <communication>\n      <api>RESTful endpoints for data processing and retrieval</api>\n      <data_format>JSON for all data exchange between frontend and backend</data_format>\n      <file_upload>Multipart/form-data for batch file upload (optional) or local file path specification</file_handling>\n    </communication>\n    <dependencies>\n      <python>\n        - flask>=2.0.0\n        - flask-cors>=3.0.10\n        - pillow>=9.0.0\n        - numpy>=1.21.0\n      </python>\n      <frontend_cdn>\n        - Chart.js v4.4.0\n        - Bootstrap 5.3.0 (optional)\n        - Font Awesome 6.4.0\n      </frontend_cdn>\n    </dependencies>\n  </technology_stack>\n\n  <prerequisites>\n    <environment_setup>\n      - Python 3.8+ installed on the system\n      - Flask and required dependencies installed via pip: pip install flask flask-cors pillow numpy\n      - Local dataset organized in a structured directory (images in /images, ground truth JSON in /gt, predictions JSON in /predictions)\n      - Backend code in /app directory with app.py as entry point\n      - Frontend assets (HTML/CSS/JS) in /app/static directory\n      - Template files in /app/templates directory\n      - Environment variables (optional) for dataset path configuration (.env file with DATASET_PATH)\n    </environment_setup>\n    <dataset_format>\n      <image_sequence>\n        - All images in a single directory (JPG/PNG format) with consistent naming convention (e.g., img_001.jpg, img_002.png)\n        - Image dimensions consistent or variable (tool should handle both)\n      </image_sequence>\n      <ground_truth_json>\n        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001.json)\n        - Structure: {\n            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n            \"width\": 1920,\n            \"height\": 1080,\n            \"annotations\": [\n              {\n                \"class\": \"car\",\n                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2]  # pixel coordinates (top-left, bottom-right)\n              },\n              ...\n            ]\n          }\n      </ground_truth_json>\n      <prediction_json>\n        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001_pred.json)\n        - Structure: {\n            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n            \"width\": 1920,\n            \"height\": 1080,\n            \"predictions\": [\n              {\n                \"class\": \"car\",\n                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2],\n                \"score\": 0.95  # confidence score (0-1)\n              },\n              ...\n            ]\n          }\n      </prediction_json>\n    </dataset_format>\n  </prerequisites>\n\n  <core_features>\n    <file_handling>\n      - Local dataset path configuration (input field for directory path)\n      - Validation of dataset structure (check for images, GT JSON, prediction JSON)\n      - Batch parsing of all files in the dataset directory\n      - Error handling for missing files, invalid JSON formats, and mismatched filenames\n      - Thumbnail generation for all images (150x150px, aspect ratio preserved)\n      - Caching of parsed data to avoid reprocessing on page refresh\n    </file_handling>\n\n    <statistics_dashboard>\n      <metrics_calculation>\n        - **Recall (True Positive Rate)**: TP / (TP + FN) per class\n        - **Precision**: TP / (TP + FP) per class\n        - **False Positive Rate (FPR)**: FP / (FP + TN) per class\n        - **F1 Score**: 2 * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall) per class\n        - **Overall Accuracy**: (TP + TN) / (TP + TN + FP + FN)\n        - **Average Precision (AP)** per class (optional)\n        - **Intersection over Union (IoU)** threshold configuration (default: 0.5) for TP/FP/FN classification\n      </metrics_calculation>\n      <visualization>\n        - Bar charts for per-class recall, precision, FPR\n        - Pie charts for class distribution in ground truth vs predictions\n        - Summary table with all metrics for easy comparison\n        - Sortable and filterable metric table (by class name, metric value)\n        - Export statistics to CSV/JSON format\n        - Interactive tooltips on charts showing exact metric values\n      </visualization>\n      <user_interface>\n        - Dropdown for IoU threshold adjustment (0.3 to 0.9 in 0.1 increments)\n        - Class filter (show/hide specific classes in charts/tables)\n        - Confidence score threshold filter for predictions (0.0 to 1.0 slider)\n        - Reset filters button to restore default settings\n        - Summary card with key overall metrics (total images, total classes, average recall/precision)\n      </user_interface>\n    </statistics_dashboard>\n\n    <image_comparison_view>\n      <left_panel>\n        - Searchable and filterable file list (by filename, class presence)\n        - Image thumbnails alongside filenames (150x150px)\n        - Scrollable list with fixed height (occupies 100% of viewport height)\n        - Highlight active/selected image in the list\n        - Pagination (optional) for large datasets (10/20/50 images per page)\n        - Class filter (show only images containing specific classes)\n        - Status filter (show only images with FP/FN/perfect detections)\n      </left_panel>\n      <right_panel>\n        <image_display>\n          - High-resolution image view (scaled to fit viewport, maintain aspect ratio)\n          - Interactive canvas overlay for bounding boxes\n          - Bounding box styles:\n            - True Positive (TP): Green border (2px), green checkmark (✓) at top-left corner\n            - False Positive (FP): Red border (2px), red cross (✗) at top-left corner\n            - False Negative (FN): Red border (2px), red horizontal dash (—) at top-left corner\n          - Bounding box labels (class name + confidence score for predictions)\n          - Zoom/pan functionality for detailed inspection\n          - Toggle visibility of ground truth/prediction boxes\n          - Toggle visibility of box labels/indicators\n        </image_display>\n        <per_image_statistics>\n          - Summary card for current image (filename, dimensions, total GT boxes, total predicted boxes)\n          - Per-class breakdown table (GT count, predicted count, TP, FP, FN for each class)\n          - IoU values for each matched bounding box (optional tooltip on hover)\n          - Confidence score distribution for predictions on current image\n          - Navigation buttons (previous/next image) for sequential viewing\n        </per_image_statistics>\n      </right_panel>\n    </image_comparison_view>\n\n    <navigation>\n      - Top navigation bar with links to Statistics Dashboard and Image Comparison View\n      - Active page indicator in navigation bar\n      - Breadcrumb navigation for context (current dataset path, current image)\n      - Back to top button for long pages (statistics dashboard)\n      - Responsive navigation (collapsible menu on mobile devices)\n    </navigation>\n\n    <error_handling>\n      - User-friendly error messages for invalid dataset paths\n      - Validation errors for malformed JSON files (line number + error description)\n      - Warning messages for mismatched filenames (GT/prediction JSON without corresponding image)\n      - Loading spinners during data processing/file parsing\n      - Empty state handling (no data loaded, no images to display)\n      - Fallback UI for unsupported image formats\n    </error_handling>\n\n    <accessibility>\n      - Keyboard navigation (Tab/Enter for list selection, arrow keys for image navigation)\n      - Alt text for all images and icons\n      - High contrast mode for bounding boxes (optional toggle)\n      - Screen reader compatible labels for all UI elements\n      - Responsive design for mobile/tablet/desktop viewing\n      - Text size adjustment option (small/medium/large)\n    </accessibility>\n  </core_features>\n\n  <database_schema>\n    <tables>\n      <dataset_metadata>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - path (text, unique)\n        - total_images (integer)\n        - total_classes (integer)\n        - iou_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n        - confidence_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n        - created_at (timestamp)\n        - last_updated (timestamp)\n      </dataset_metadata>\n\n      <image_metadata>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n        - filename (text)\n        - width (integer)\n        - height (integer)\n        - thumbnail_path (text)\n        - total_gt_boxes (integer)\n        - total_pred_boxes (integer)\n        - has_fp (boolean)\n        - has_fn (boolean)\n        - is_perfect (boolean)\n      </image_metadata>\n\n      <classes>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n        - name (text, unique per dataset)\n        - total_gt_count (integer)\n        - total_pred_count (integer)\n        - tp_count (integer)\n        - fp_count (integer)\n        - fn_count (integer)\n        - recall (float)\n        - precision (float)\n        - fpr (float)\n        - f1_score (float)\n      </classes>\n\n      <bounding_boxes>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - image_id (foreign key to image_metadata.id)\n        - class_id (foreign key to classes.id)\n        - type (text, enum: 'ground_truth', 'prediction')\n        - x1 (float)\n        - y1 (float)\n        - x2 (float)\n        - y2 (float)\n        - confidence (float, null for ground truth)\n        - iou (float, null for unmatched boxes)\n        - classification (text, enum: 'tp', 'fp', 'fn', null for unclassified)\n      </bounding_boxes>\n    </tables>\n    <notes>\n      - Database is SQLite (file-based) for simplicity, stored as dataset_analysis.db\n      - Data is cleared/overwritten when a new dataset is loaded\n      - Indexes on filename, class name, and image_id for faster queries\n    </notes>\n  </database_schema>\n\n  <api_endpoints_summary>\n    <dataset>\n      - classFilter.remove(1);\n   142→        }\n   143→\n   144→        // Add class options\n   145→        this.allClasses.forEach(cls => {\n   146→            const option = document.createElement('option');\n   147→            option.value = cls.name;\n   148→            option.textContent = cls.name;\n   149→            classFilter.appendChild(option);\n   150→        });\n   151→    }\n   152→\n   153→    async loadImagesList() {\n   154→        if (!this.datasetId) return;\n   155→\n   156→        try {\n   157→            // Build URL with filter parameters (class and status filters are server-side)\n   158→            let url = `/api/images/${this.datasetId}?per_page=50`;\n   159→\n   160→            if (this.filters.classFilter) {\n   161→                url += `&class_filter=${encodeURIComponent(this.filters.classFilter)}`;\n   162→            }\n   163→\n   164→            if (this.filters.statusFilter) {\n   165→                url += 175→        } catch (error) {\n   176→            console.error('Error loading images list:', error);\n   177→            const container = document.getElementById('image-list-container');\n   178→            if (container) {\n   179→                container.innerHTML = '<div class=\"text-center text-danger py-5\">Failed to load images</div>';\n   180→            }\n   181→        }\n   182→    }\n   183→\n   184→    applyClientSideFilters() {\n   185→        if (!this.allImages) return;\n   186→\n   187→        let filteredImages = [...this.allImages];\n   188→\n   189→        // Apply 198→        this.renderImagesList(filteredImages);\n   199→    }\n   200→\n   201→    renderImagesList(images) {\n   202→        const container = document.getElementById('image-list-container');\n 'status-warning' : 'status-perfect');\n   212→            return `\n   213→                <div class=\"image-list-item\" data-image-id=\"${image.id}\">\n   214→                    <img src=\"${image.thumbnail_path || ''}\" alt=\"${this.escapeHtml(image.filename)}\" class=\"thumbnail\" onerror=\"this.src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22 width=%2260%22 height=%2260%22%3E%3Crect fill=%22%23e2e8f0%22 width=%22100%25%22 height=%22100%25%22/%3E%3Ctext fill=%22%2394a3b8%22 x=%2250%25%22 y=%2250%25%22 text-anchor=%22middle%22 dy=%22.3em%22%3E%3F%3C/text%3E%3C/svg%3E'\">\n   215→                    <div class=\"image-info\">\n   216→                        <div class=\"filename\">${this.escapeHtml(image.filename)}</div>\n   217→                        <div class=\"image-stats\">\n   218→                            GT: ${image.total_gt_boxes} | Pred: ${image.total_pred_boxes}\n   219→                        </div>\n   220→                    </div>\n   221→                    <span class=\"status-dot ${statusClass}\" title=\"${image.is_perfect ?       container.querySelectorAll('.image-list-item').forEach(item => {\n   228→            item.addEventListener('click', () => {\n   229→                const imageId = if (prevBtn) {\n   445→            prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.navigateImage(-1));\n   446→        }\n   447→        if (nextBtn) {\n   448→            nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.navigateImage(1));\n   449→        }\n   450→\n   451→        // Store current image data for re-rendering\n   452→        this.currentImageData = data;\n this.setupToggleButtons();\n   459→\n   460→        // Add event listeners for zoom controls\n   461→        this.setupZoomControls();\n   462→\n   463→        // Add event listeners for pan/drag functionality\n   464→        this.setupPanDrag();\n   465→    }\n   466→\n   467→    renderImageWithBoundingBoxes(data) {\n   468→        const canvas = document.getElementById('image-canvas');\n   469→        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n   470→        if (!canvas || !ctx) return;\n   471→\n   472→        // Set canvas dimensions\n   473→        const width = data.dimensions?.width || 800;\n   474→        const height = data.dimensions?.height || 600;\n   475→        canvas.width = width;\n   476→        canvas.height = height;\n   477→\n   478→        // Clear canvas and apply zoom/pan transforms\n   479→        ctx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);\n   480→        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);\n   481→\n   482→        // Apply zoom and pan transformations\n   483→        ctx.translate(this.panX, this.panY);\n   484→        ctx.scale(this.zoomLevel, this.zoomLevel);\n   485→\n   486→        // Create a placeholder image (since we don't have actual image files)\n   487→        // In a real implementation, you would load the actual image file\n   488→        this.drawPlaceholderImage(ctx, width, height);\n   489→\n   490→        // Draw bounding boxes\n   491→        const gtBoxes = data.ground_truth_boxes || [];\n   492→        const predBoxes = data.prediction_boxes || [];\n   493→\n   494→        // Combine all boxes for rendering\n   495→        // FN boxes are GT boxes without matching prediction (classification is null)\n   496→        const fnBoxes = gtBoxes.filter(box => box.classification === null);\n   497→        // FP boxes are prediction boxes without matching GT\n   498→        const fpBoxes = predBoxes.filter(box => box.classification === 'fp');\n   499→        // TP boxes are matched predictions (classification is 'tp')\n   500→        const tpBoxes = predBoxes.filter(box => box.classification === 'tp');\n   501→\n   502→        // Draw GT boxes (FN only, since TP are predictions that match GT)\n   503→        if (this.showGTBoxes) {\n   504→            fnBoxes.forEach(box => this.drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, 'fn'));\n   505→        }\n   506→\n   507→        // Draw prediction boxes (FP and TP)\n   508→        if (this.showPredBoxes) {\n   509→            fpBoxes.forEach(box => this.drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, 'fp'));\n   510→            tpBoxes.forEach(box => this.drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, 'tp'));\n   511→        }\n   512→    }\n   513→\n   514→    drawPlaceholderImage(ctx, width, height) {\n   515→        // Draw a gradient background\n   516→        const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, width, height);\n   517→        gradient.addColorStop(0, '#f0f9ff');\n   518→        gradient.addColorStop(1, '#e0f2fe');\n   519→        ctx.fillStyle = gradient;\n   520→        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n   521→\n   522→        // Draw some placeholder shapes to simulate an image\n   523→        ctx.strokeStyle = '#cbd5e1';\n   524→        ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n   525→\n   526→        // Draw a grid\n   527→        for (let x = 0; x < width; x += 50) {\n   528→            ctx.beginPath();\n   529→            ctx.moveTo(x, 0);\n   530→            ctx.lineTo(x, height);\n   531→            ctx.stroke();\n   532→        }\n   533→        for (let y = 0; y < height; y += 50) {\n   534→            ctx.beginPath();\n   535→            ctx.moveTo(0, y);\n   536→            ctx.lineTo(width, y);\n   537→            ctx.stroke();\n   538→        }\n   539→\n   540→        // Draw placeholder text\n   541→        ctx.fillStyle = '#94a3b8';\n   542→        ctx.font = '24px Inter, sans-serif';\n   543→        ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n   544→        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n   545→        ctx.fillText('Image Placeholder', width / 2, height / 2);\n   546→        ctx.font = '14px Inter, sans-serif';\n   547→        ctx.fillText(`${width} x ${height}`, width / 2, height / 2 + 30);\n   548→    }\n   549→\n   550→    drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, type) {\n   551→        const bbox = box.bbox;\n   552→        if (!bbox || bbox.length !== 4) return;\n   553→\n   554→        const [x1, y1, x2, y2] = bbox;\n   555→        const width = x2 - x1;\n   556→        const height = y2 - y1;\n   557→\n   558→        // Set style based on type\n   559→        let color, lineWidth;\n   560→        switch (type) {\n   561→            case 'tp':\n   562→                color = '#22c55e'; // green\n   563→                lineWidth = 2;\n   564→                break;\n   565→            case 'fp':\n   566→                color = '#ef4444'; // red\n   567→                lineWidth = 2;\n   568→                break;\n   569→            case 'fn':\n   570→                color = '#ef4444'; // red\n   571→                lineWidth = 2;\n   572→                break;\n   573→            default:\n   574→                return;\n   575→        }\n   576→\n   577→        // Draw bounding box\n   578→        ctx.strokeStyle = color;\n   579→        ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth;\n   580→\n   581→        if (type === 'fn') {\n   582→            ctx.setLineDash([5, 3]); // Dashed line for FN\n   583→        } else {\n   584→            ctx.setLineDash([]);\n   585→        }\n   586→\n   587→        ctx.strokeRect(x1, y1, width, height);\n   588→        ctx.setLineDash([]); // Reset dash\n   589→\n   590→        // Draw corner indicator (24x24px square at top-left)\n   591→        const indicatorSize = 24;\n   592→        const indicatorX = x1 - 2;\n   593→        const indicatorY = y1 - 12;\n   594→        const centerX = indicatorX + indicatorSize / 2;\n   595→        const centerY = indicatorY + indicatorSize / 2;\n   596→\n   597→        ctx.fillStyle = color;\n   598→        ctx.fillRect(indicatorX, indicatorY, indicatorSize, indicatorSize);\n   599→\n   600→        // Draw icon in the corner indicator using canvas paths instead of text\n   601→        ctx.fillStyle = 'white';\n   602→        ctx.strokeStyle = 'white';\n   603→        ctx.lineWidth = 2;\n   604→\n   605→        if (type === 'tp') {\n   606→            // Draw checkmark (✓)\n   607→            ctx.beginPath();\n   608→            ctx.moveTo(centerX - 4, centerY);\n   609→            ctx.lineTo(centerX, centerY + 4);\n   610→            ctx.lineTo(centerX + 6, centerY - 6);\n   611→            ctx.stroke();\n   612→        } else if (type === 'fp') {\n   613→            // Draw cross (✗)\n   614→            ctx.beginPath();\n   615→            ctx.moveTo(centerX - 4, centerY - 4);\n   616→            ctx.lineTo(centerX + 4, centerY + 4);\n   617→            ctx.moveTo(centerX + 4, centerY - 4);\n   618→            ctx.lineTo(centerX - 4, centerY + 4);\n   619→            ctx.stroke();\n   620→        } else if (type === 'fn') {\n   621→            // Draw dash (—)\n   622→            ctx.beginPath();\n   623→            ctx.moveTo(centerX - 6, centerY);\n   624→            ctx.lineTo(centerX + 6, centerY);\n   625→            ctx.stroke();\n   626→        }\n   627→\n   628→        // Draw label (class name and confidence for predictions)\n   629→        if (this.showLabels) {\n   630→            let labelText = '';\n   631→            if (box.class_name) {\n   632→                labelText = box.class_name;\n   633→            }\n   634→            if (box.confidence !== undefined && box.confidence !== null) {\n   635→                labelText += ` (${box.confidence.toFixed(2)})`;\n   636→            }\n   637→\n   638→            if (labelText) {\n   639→                ctx.font = '11px Inter, sans-serif';\n   640→                const textMetrics = ctx.measureText(labelText);\n   641→                const labelWidth = textMetrics.width + 12;\n   642→                const labelHeight = 20;\n   643→\n   644→                // Draw label background (semi-transparent)\n   645→                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.7)';\n   646→                ctx.fillRect(x1, y1 + 12, labelWidth, labelHeight);\n   647→\n   648→                // Draw label text\n   649→                ctx.fillStyle = 'white';\n   650→                ctx.textAlign = 'left';\n   651→                ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n   652→                ctx.fillText(labelText, x1 + 6, y1 + 22);\n   653→            }\n   654→        }\n   655→    }\n   656→\n   657→    setupToggleButtons() {\n   658→        // GT Boxes toggle\n   659→        const gtToggle = document.getElementById('toggle-gt-boxes');\n   660→        if (gtToggle) {\n   661→            gtToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {\n   662→                this.showGTBoxes = !this.showGTBoxes;\n   663→                gtToggle.classList.toggle('active');\n   664→                this.reRenderCurrentImage();\n   665→            });\n   666→        }\n   667→\n   668→        // Prediction Boxes toggle\n   669→        const predToggle = document.getElementById('toggle-pred-boxes');\n   670→        if (predToggle) {\n   671→            predToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {\n   672→                this.showPredBoxes = !this.showPredBoxes;\n   673→                predToggle.classList.toggle('active');\n   674→ }\n   739→\n   740→    setupPanDrag() {\n   741→        const canvas = document.getElementById('image-canvas');\n   742→        const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');\n   743→        if (!canvas || !container) return;\n   744→\n   745→        // Reset pan on new image load\n   746→        this.panX = 0;\n   747→        this.panY = 0;\n   748→\n   749→        // Update cursor       if (this.zoomLevel === 1.0) return; // Only allow panning when zoomed\n   755→\n   756→            this.isDragging = true;\n   757→            this.dragStartX = e.clientX;\n   758→            this.dragStartY = e.clientY;\n   759→        });\n   760→\n   761→        // Mouse move - update pan position\n   762→        canvas.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {\n   763→            if dx;\n   769→            this.panY += dy;\n   770→\n   771→            this.dragStartX = e.clientX;\n   772→            this.dragStartY = e.clientY;\n   773→\n   774→            this.reRenderCurrentImage();\n   775→        });\n   776→\n   777→        // Mouse up - stop dragging\n   778→        canvas.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {\n   779→            this.isDragging =      });\n   786→    }\n   787→\n   788→    updateCanvasCursor() {\n   789→        const canvas = document.getElementById('image-canvas');\n   790→        if (!canvas) return;\n   791→\n   792→ 798→\n   799→    navigateImage(direction) {\n   800→        const items = document.querySelectorAll('.image-list-item');\n   801→        if (items.length === 0) return;\n   802→\n   803→        let setupSortableTableHeaders() {\n   930→        // Store current sort state\n   931→        this.currentSort = {\n   932→            column: null,\n   933→            direction: 'asc'\n   934→        };\n   935→\n   936→        // Get all sortable headers\n   937→        const sortableHeaders = document.querySelectorAll('th.sortable');\n   938→        sortableHeaders.forEach(header => {\n   939→            header.addEventListener('click', () => {\n   940→                const sortColumn = header.getAttribute('data-sort');\n   941→                const sortType = header.getAttribute('data-type');\n   942→\n   943→                // Toggle sort direction if clicking same column\n   944→                if (this.currentSort.column === sortColumn) {\n   945→                    this.currentSort.direction = this.currentSort.direction === 'asc' ? 'desc' : 'asc';\n   946→                } else {\n   947→                    this.currentSort.column = sortColumn;\n   948→                    this.currentSort.direction = 'asc';\n   949→                }\n   950→\n   951→                // Update sort icons\n   952→                this.updateSortIcons();\n   953→\n   954→                // Sort the table\n   955→                this.sortMetricsTable(sortColumn, sortType, this.currentSort.direction);\n   956→            });\n   957→        });\n   958→    }\n   959→\n   960→    updateSortIcons() {\n   961→        // Clear all sort icons\n   962→        const allIcons = document.querySelectorAll('.sort-icon');\n   963→        allIcons.forEach(icon => {\n   964→            icon.innerHTML = '';\n   965→        });\n   966→\n   967→        // Set icon for current sort column\n   968→        if (this.currentSort.column) {\n   969→            const header = document.querySelector(`th[data-sort=\"${this.currentSort.column}\"]`);\n   970→            if (header) {\n   971→                const icon = header.querySelector('.sort-icon');\n   972→                if (icon) {\n   973→                    icon.innerHTML = this.currentSort.direction === 'asc' ? '&#9650;' : '&#9660;'; // Up or down arrow\n   974→                }\n   975→            }\n   976→        }\n   977→    }\n   978→\n   979→    sortMetricsTable(column, type, direction) {\n   980→        const tableBody = document.getElementById('metrics-table-body');\n   981→        if (!tableBody) return;\n   982→\n   983→        const rows = Array.from(tableBody.querySelectorAll('tr'));\n   984→\n   985→        // Get column index\n   986→        const headerIndex = this.getColumnIndex(column);\n   987→        if (headerIndex === -1) return;\n   988→\n   989→        // Sort rows\n   990→        rows.sort((rowA, rowB) => {\n   991→            const cellA = rowA.cells[headerIndex];\n   992→            const cellB = rowB.cells[headerIndex];\n   993→\n   994→            if (!cellA || !cellB) return 0;\n   995→\n   996→            let valueA, valueB;\n   997→\n   998→            if (type === 'string') {\n   999→                valueA = cellA.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();\n  1000→                valueB = cellB.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();\n  1001→            } else {\n  1002→                // For numeric values, remove formatting and parse\n  1003→                valueA = parseFloat(cellA.textContent.replace(/[^\\d.-]/g, '')) || 0;\n  1004→                valueB = parseFloat(cellB.textContent.replace(/[^\\d.-]/g, '')) || 0;\n  1005→            }\n  1006→\n  1007→            if (valueA < valueB) return direction === 'asc' ? -1 : 1;\n  1008→            if (valueA > valueB) return direction === 'asc' ? 1 : -1;\n  1009→            return 0;\n  1010→        });\n  1011→\n  1012→        // Reorder rows in the table\n  1013→        rows.forEach(row => {\n  1014→            tableBody.appendChild(row);\n  1015→        });\n  1016→    }\n  1017→\n  1018→    getColumnIndex(columnName) {\n  1019→        const headers = document.querySelectorAll('th[data-sort]');\n  1020→        for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {\n  1021→            if (headers[i].getAttribute('data-sort') === columnName) {\n  1022→                return i;\n  1023→            }\n  1024→        }\n  1025→        return -1;\n  1026→    }\n  1027→\n  1028→    updateSliderTrackFill(slider) {\n  1029→        // Calculate the percentage of the slider value\n  1030→        const min = parseFloat(slider.min) || 0;\n  1031→        const max = parseFloat(slider.max) || 1;\n  1032→        const value = parseFloat(slider.value) || 0;\n  1033→        const percentage = ((value - min) / (max - min)) * 100;\n  1034→\n  1035→        // Update the background gradient for track fill effect\n  1036→        const primaryColor = '#2c5282';\n  1037→        const trackColor = '#e2e8f0';\n  1038→        slider.style.background = `linear-gradient(to right, ${primaryColor} 0%, ${primaryColor} ${percentage}%, ${trackColor} ${percentage}%, ${trackColor} 100%)`;\n  1039→    }\n  1040→\n  1041→    showLoadDatasetModal() {\n  1042→        // TODO: Implement load dataset modal\n  1043→        console.log('Load dataset modal');\n  1044→    }\n  1045→\n  1046→    async loadDataset(path) {\n  1047→        try {\n  1048→            this.showLoading();\n  1049→\n  1050→            const response = await fetch('/api/dataset/load', {\n  1051→                method: 'POST',\n  1052→                headers: {\n  1053→                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n  1054→                },\n  1055→                body: JSON.stringify({\n  1056→                    dataset_path: path,\n  1057→                    iou_threshold: this.iouThreshold\n  1058→                })\n  1059→            });\n  1060→\n  1061→            const data = await response.json();\n  1062→\n  1063→            if (data.success) {\n  1064→                this.datasetId = data.dataset_id;\n  1065→                window.location.hash = '#dashboard';\n  1066→                await this.loadStatistics();\n  1067→            } else {\n  1068→                this.showError('Failed to load dataset');\n  1069→            }\n  1070→        } catch (error) {\n  1071→            this.showError('Error loading dataset: ' + error.message);\n  1072→        } finally {\n  1073→            this.hideLoading();\n  1074→        }\n  1075→    }\n  1076→\n  1077→    async loadStatistics() {\n  1078→        try {\n  1079→            const response display state\n  1083→            this.showDashboard();\n  1084→        } catch (error) {\n  1085→            this.showError('Error loading statistics');\n  1086→        }\n  1087→    }\n  1088→\n  1089→    updateDashboard(data) {\n  1090→        // Update summary cards\n  1091→        if (data.overall_metrics) {\n  1092→            document.getElementById('summary-total-images').textContent = data.overall_metrics.total_gt_boxes || '-';\n  1093→            document.getElementById('summary-total-classes').textContent = data.classes?.length || '-';\n  1094→            document.getElementById('summary-avg-recall').textContent = data.overall_metrics.recall !== undefined ? data.overall_metrics.recall.toFixed(3) : '-';\n  1095→            document.getElementById('summary-avg-precision').textContent = data.overall_metrics.precision !== undefined ? data.overall_metrics.precision.toFixed(3) : '-';\n  1096→        }\n  1097→\n  1098→        // Update metrics table\n  1099→        this.updateMetricsTable(data.classes || []);\n  1100→\n  1101→        // Update charts\n  1102→        this.updateCharts(data.classes || []);\n  1103→    }\n  1104→\n  1105→    updateMetricsTable(classes) {\n  1106→        const tableBody = document.getElementById('metrics-table-body');\n  1107→        if (!tableBody) return;\n  1108→\n  1109→        if (classes.length === 0) {\n  1110→            tableBody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan=\"10\" class=\"text-center text-muted\">No data available.</td></tr>';\n  1111→            return;\n  1112→        }\n  1113→\n  1114→        tableBody.innerHTML = classes.map(cls => `\n  1115→            <tr>\n  1116→                <td><strong>${this.escapeHtml(cls.name)}</strong></td>\n  1117→                <td>${cls.total_gt_count || 0}</td>\n  1118→                <td>${cls.total_pred_count || 0}</td>\n  1119→                <td>${cls.tp_count || 0}</td>\n  1120→                <td>${cls.fp_count || undefined ? cls.precision.toFixed(3) : '-'}</td>\n  1124→                <td>${cls.fpr !== undefined ? cls.fpr.toFixed(3) : '-'}</td>\n  1125→                <td>${cls.f1_score !== undefined ? cls.f1_score.toFixed(3) : '-'}</td>\n  1126→            </tr>\n  1127→        `).join('');\n  1128→    }\n  1129→\n  1130→    updateCharts(classes) {\n  1131→        if (classes.length === 0) return;\n  1132→\n  1133→        const labels = classes.map(cls => cls.name);\n  1134→        const recallData = classes.map(cls => cls.recall !== undefined ? cls.recall : 0);\n  1135→        const this.createOrUpdateChart('recall-chart', 'Recall', labels, recallData, colors);\n  1143→\n  1144→        // Update precision chart\n  1145→        this.createOrUpdateChart('precision-chart', 1149→    }\n  1150→\n  1151→    createOrUpdateChart(canvasId, label, labels, data, colors) {\n  1152→        const canvas = document.getElementById(canvasId);\n  1153→        if (!canvas) return;\n  1154→\n  1155→        // Set canvas height explicitly for Chart.js to render properly\n  1156→        canvas.style.height = '300px';\n  1157→        canvas.style.width = '100%';\n  1158→\n  1159→        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n  1160→\n  1161→        // Check if chart already exists and destroy it\n  1162→        if (canvas.chart) {\n  1163→            canvas.chart.destroy();\n  1164→        }\n  1165→\n  1166→        // Create new chart with enhanced tooltip configuration\n  1167→        canvas.chart = new Chart(ctx, {\n  1168→            type: 'bar',\n  1169→            data: {\n  1170→                labels: labels,\n  1171→                datasets: [{\n  1172→                    label: label,\n  1173→                    data: data,\n  1174→                    backgroundColor: colors.map(c => c.background),\n  1175→                    borderColor: colors.map(c => c.border),\n  1176→                    borderWidth: 2\n  1177→                }]\n  1178→            },\n  1179→            options: {\n  1180→                responsive: true,\n  1181→                maintainAspectRatio: false,\n  1182→                scales: {\n  1183→                    y: {\n  1184→                        beginAtZero: true,\n  1185→                        max: 1,\n  1186→                        grid: {\n  1187→                            color: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1)'\n  1188→                        }\n  1189→                    },\n  1190→                    x: {\n  1191→                        grid: {\n  1192→                            display: false\n  1193→                        }\n  1194→                    }\n  1195→                },\n  1196→                plugins: {\n  1197→                    legend: {\n  1198→                        display: false\n  1199→                    },\n  1200→                    tooltip: {\n  1201→                        enabled: true,\n  1202→                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)',\n  1203→                        titleColor: '#fff',\n  1204→                        bodyColor: '#fff',\n  1205→                        borderColor: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)',\n  1206→                        borderWidth: 1,\n  1207→                        padding: 12,\n  1208→                        cornerRadius: 6,\n  1209→                        callbacks: {\n  1210→                            label: function(context) {\n  1211→                                return `${context.dataset.label}: ${context.parsed.y.toFixed(3)}`;\n  1212→                            },\n  1213→                            title: function(context) {\n  1214→                                return context[0].label;\n  1215→                            }\n  1216→                        }\n  1217→                    }\n  1218→                }\n  1219→            }\n  1220→        });\n  1221→    }\n  1222→\n  1223→    generateColors(count) {\n  1224→        const colors = [];\n  1225→        const baseHues = [210, 150, 45, 0, 270, 180, 300, 330, 30, 60]; // Blue, green, orange, red, purple, cyan, magenta, pink, brown, yellow\n  1226→\n  1227→        for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {\n  1228→            const `hsla(${hue}, ${saturation}%, ${lightness}%, 0.7)`,\n  1233→                border: `hsla(${hue}, ${saturation}%, ${lightness - 10}%, 1)`\n  1234→            });\n  1235→        }\n  1236→\n  1237→        return colors;\n  1238→    }\n  1239→\n  1240→    escapeHtml(text) {\n  1241→        const div = document.createElement('div');\n  1242→        div.textContent = text;\n  1243→        return boxes without matching prediction (classification is null)\n        const fnBoxes = gtBoxes.filter(box => box.classification === null);\n        // FP boxes are prediction boxes without matching GT\n box.classification === 'tp');\n\n        // Draw GT boxes (FN only, since TP are predictions that match GT)\n        if (this.showGTBoxes) {\n            fnBoxes.forEach(box => this.drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, 'fn'));\n        }\n\n        // Draw prediction boxes (FP and TP)\n        if (this.showPredBoxes) {\n            fpBoxes.forEach(box => this.drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, 'fp'));\n            tpBoxes.forEach(box => this.drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, 'tp'));\n        }\n    }\n\n    drawPlaceholderImage(ctx, width, height) {\n        // Draw a gradient background\n        const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, width, height);\n        gradient.addColorStop(0, '#f0f9ff');\n        gradient.addColorStop(1, '#e0f2fe');\n        ctx.fillStyle = gradient;\n        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);\n\n        // Draw some placeholder shapes to simulate an image\n        ctx.strokeStyle = '#cbd5e1';\n        ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n\n        // Draw a grid\n        for (let x = 0; x < width; x += 50) {\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.moveTo(x, 0);\n            ctx.lineTo(x, height);\n            ctx.stroke();\n        }\n        for (let y = 0; y < height; y += 50) {\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.moveTo(0, y);\n            ctx.lineTo(width, y);\n            ctx.stroke();\n        }\n\n        // Draw placeholder text\n        ctx.fillStyle = '#94a3b8';\n        ctx.font = '24px Inter, sans-serif';\n        ctx.textAlign = 'center';\n        ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';\n        ctx.fillText('Image Placeholder', width / 2, height / 2);\n        ctx.font = '14px Inter, sans-serif';\n        ctx.fillText(`${width} x ${height}`, width / 2, height / 2 + 30);\n    }\n\n    drawBoundingBox(ctx, box, type) {\n        const bbox = box.bbox;\n        if (!bbox || bbox.length !== 4) return;\n\n        const [x1, y1, x2, y2] = bbox;\n        const width = x2 - x1;\n        const height = y2 - y1;\n\n        // Set style based on type\n        let color, lineWidth;\n        switch (type) {\n            case 'tp':\n                color = '#22c55e'; // green\n                lineWidth = 2;\n                break;\n            case 'fp':\n                color = '#ef4444'; // red\n                lineWidth = 2;\n                break;\n            case 'fn':\n                color = '#ef4444'; // red\n                lineWidth = 2;\n                break;\n            default:\n                return;\n        }\n\n        // Draw bounding box\n        ctx.strokeStyle = color;\n        ctx.lineWidth = lineWidth;\n\n        if (type === 'fn') {\n            ctx.setLineDash([5, 3]); // Dashed line for FN\n        } else {\n            ctx.setLineDash([]);\n        }\n\n        ctx.strokeRect(x1, y1, width, height);\n        ctx.setLineDash([]); // Reset dash\n\n        // Draw corner indicator (24x24px square at top-left)\n        const indicatorSize = 24;\n        const indicatorX = x1 - 2;\n        const indicatorY = y1 - 12;\n        const centerX = indicatorX + indicatorSize / 2;\n        const centerY = indicatorY + indicatorSize / 2;\n\n        ctx.fillStyle = color;\n        ctx.fillRect(indicatorX, indicatorY, indicatorSize, indicatorSize);\n\n        // Draw icon in the corner indicator using canvas paths instead of text\n        ctx.fillStyle = 'white';\n        ctx.strokeStyle = 'white';\n        ctx.lineWidth = 2;\n\n        if (type === 'tp') {\n            // Draw checkmark (✓)\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.moveTo(centerX - 4, centerY);\n            ctx.lineTo(centerX, centerY + 4);\n            ctx.lineTo(centerX + 6, centerY - 6);\n            ctx.stroke();\n        } else if (type === 'fp') {\n            // Draw cross (✗)\n
